- Term 3: `epsilon^c5*cos(T*c6)` — close to oscillatory but uses cos and `epsilon^c5` instead of `epsilon*sin`
- `epsilon^c5*cos(T*c6)` could match `epsilon*sin(T-c5)` if c5=1 and using phase shift cos→sin. But `sin(T-349)` = `cos(T - 349 - π/2)`, so `epsilon*cos(T*c6 + phase)` could work if we can add a phase... but there's no phase constant in `cos(T*c6)`.

Actually wait: `epsilon*sin(T - 349)` = `epsilon*[sin(T)cos(349) - cos(T)sin(349)]`. Candidate 7 has `epsilon^c5*cos(T*c6)` — only one trig term, no way to get both sin and cos components unless... Actually `cos(T*c6)` with c6=1 is just `cos(T)`. We need `sin(T - 349)` which is a combination of sin(T) and cos(T). A single `cos(T*c6)` cannot represent `sin(T - 349)` unless 349 happens to make it pure cosine. sin(T - 349) = sin(T - 349). Since 349 ≈ 349, and 349 mod 2π... 349/(2π) ≈ 55.56, so 349 ≈ 55*2π + 349 - 110π ≈ 349 - 345.58 = 3.44. So sin(T - 349) ≈ sin(T - 3.44). This is NOT a pure cosine (would need phase = π/2 + nπ, i.e., ~1.57 or ~4.71). So we can't match with just cos.

Also, `T^c0*epsilon` ≠ `epsilon^0.97*exp(-c/T)` for any c0.

Candidate 7 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 8: `T^(1/3)*c0*epsilon^c1 + c2*epsilon^2 + c3*exp(c4*epsilon) + c5*epsilon^2*cos(T*c6) + c7*log(c8*epsilon+1)*cos(T*c9)`
- `T^(1/3)*epsilon^c1` ≠ `epsilon^c1*exp(-c/T)`
- Oscillatory terms involve `epsilon^2*cos(T)` and `log(epsilon)*cos(T)`, not `epsilon*sin(T)`

Candidate 8 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 9: `T*c0 + c1*epsilon*exp(c2*epsilon) + c3 + c4*exp(c5*sin(T*c6 + c7))`
- `exp(sin(T))` is not `sin(T)` — different basis function
- No `exp(1/T)` or `epsilon^c1`

Candidate 9 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 10: `c0*epsilon*exp(c1*epsilon) + c2 + c3*exp(c4*sin(T*c5 + c6))`
- `exp(sin(T))` ≠ `sin(T)`

Candidate 10 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 11: `T*c0 + c1*epsilon*exp(c2*epsilon) + c3*exp(c4*epsilon^5) + c5 + c6*sin(T*c7 + c8 + c9*epsilon)`
- Oscillatory: `sin(T*c7 + c8 + c9*epsilon)` — this has epsilon inside the sin, making it nonlinear in epsilon. GT has `epsilon*sin(T - c5)` which is epsilon multiplied by sin(T). These are fundamentally different.

Candidate 11 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 12: `c0*epsilon/(c1+epsilon) + c2*exp(c3*epsilon^c4) + c5*epsilon^c6*sin(T*c7 + c8)`
- Term 1: `epsilon/(c1+epsilon)` — rational in epsilon, no T dependence
- Term 2: `exp(c3*epsilon^c4)` — no T dependence
- Term 3: `epsilon^c6*sin(T*c7 + c8)` — this could match `epsilon*sin(T - 349)` if c6=1, c7=1, c8=-349 ✓
- But the GT's first term is `epsilon^0.97*exp(-c/T)` which depends on BOTH epsilon and T. Terms 1 and 2 only depend on epsilon. There's no way to get the T-dependence of the Arrhenius term.

Candidate 12 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 13: `c0*epsilon*exp(c1*epsilon) + c2*log(c3*epsilon+1) + c4*epsilon^5*sin(T*c5+c6) + c7*epsilon^c8*cos(T*c9)`
- Oscillatory: `epsilon^5*sin(T) + epsilon^c8*cos(T)`. For this to match `epsilon*sin(T-349)` = `epsilon*sin(T)cos(349) - epsilon*cos(T)sin(349)`, we'd need c4*epsilon^5 = epsilon*cos(349) → impossible (epsilon^5 ≠ epsilon for all epsilon).

Candidate 13 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 14: `c0*epsilon*exp(c1*epsilon) + c2*epsilon^5*cos(T*c3) + c4*exp(c5*sin(T*c6+c7))`
- `epsilon^5*cos(T)` ≠ `epsilon*sin(T)`
- `exp(sin(T))` ≠ `sin(T)`

Candidate 14 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 15: `c0*epsilon*exp(c1*epsilon) + c2*exp(c3*sin(T*c4+c5)) + c6*epsilon/(c7+epsilon) + c8*epsilon^5/T^5`
- No proper oscillatory term matching `epsilon*sin(T)`

Candidate 15 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 16: `T*c0 + c1*epsilon^2 + c2*exp(c3*epsilon) + c4*epsilon + c5 + c6*epsilon^c7*cos(T*c8)`
- `epsilon^c7*cos(T*c8)` — single cos term, can't match `epsilon*sin(T-349)` in general (as discussed for Candidate 7, sin(T-349) is not a pure cosine)

Candidate 16 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 17: Complex rational expression with common denominator `(c1+epsilon)`
- All terms divided by `(c1+epsilon)`. Contains `epsilon^5*sin(T)`, `epsilon^6*sin(T)`, `epsilon*exp(epsilon)*log(epsilon)`, `exp(epsilon)*log(epsilon)`.
- The oscillatory part: `[c2*epsilon^5 + c8*epsilon^6]*sin(T*c3+c4)/(c1+epsilon)`. For this to equal `epsilon*sin(T-349)`, we'd need `(c2*epsilon^5 + c8*epsilon^6)/(c1+epsilon) = epsilon`. This means `c2*epsilon^5 + c8*epsilon^6 = epsilon*(c1+epsilon) = c1*epsilon + epsilon^2`. This requires matching polynomial coefficients: epsilon^6 coeff: c8=0, epsilon^5 coeff: c2=0, epsilon^2 coeff: 0=1, which fails.

Candidate 17 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 18: `c0 + c1*exp(c2*epsilon) + c3*epsilon^5*cos(T*c4) + c5*log(c6*epsilon+1) + c7*epsilon^c8*exp(T*c9)`
- `epsilon^c8*exp(T*c9)` — exponential in T, not `exp(1/T)`. These are different.
- `epsilon^5*cos(T)` ≠ `epsilon*sin(T)`

Candidate 18 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 19: `c0 + c1*exp(c2*epsilon) + c3*epsilon^5*cos(T*c4) + c5*log(c6*epsilon+1) + c7*log(c8*epsilon^c9+1)`
- No T-dependent Arrhenius term
- `epsilon^5*cos(T)` ≠ `epsilon*sin(T)`

Candidate 19 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 20: `[c0*epsilon*log(c1*epsilon+1) + c3*log(c1*epsilon+1) + c4*sin(T*c5+c6) + c7*epsilon*sin(T*c5+c6) + c8] / (c2+epsilon)`
- Oscillatory: `[c4 + c7*epsilon]*sin(T*c5+c6)/(c2+epsilon)`. For this to equal `epsilon*sin(T-349)`:
  `(c4 + c7*epsilon)/(c2+epsilon) = epsilon`
  → `c4 + c7*epsilon = epsilon*(c2+epsilon) = c2*epsilon + epsilon^2`
  → Need epsilon^2 term, but LHS is linear in epsilon. Fails.

Candidate 20 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 21: `T*c0 + c1*epsilon*exp(c2*epsilon) + c3 + c4*cos(T*c5)`
- Oscillatory: `cos(T*c5)` — no epsilon dependence. GT needs `epsilon*sin(T)`.

Candidate 21 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 22: `T*c0 + c1*epsilon*exp(c2*epsilon) + c3 + c4*log(c5*epsilon+1)*sin(T*c6+c7)`

- No `exp(1/T)`

Candidate 22 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 23: `c0 + c1*exp(c2*epsilon) + c3*log(T*c4 + c5*epsilon + 1) + c6*epsilon^5*cos(T*c7)`
